| 0:27:57| substance use, and homelessness.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1677)|
| 0:27:59| How are we even defining an emergency?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1679)|
| 0:28:02| Some would define an emergency as an urgent, sudden, and serious event| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1682)|
| 0:28:05| or unforeseen change in circumstances that necessitates immediate action| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1685)|
| 0:28:09| to remedy harm or avert imminent danger to life, health, or property.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1689)|
| 0:28:14| By this definition, an emergency related to mental health is a person who is a harm to themselves or others,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1694)|
| 0:28:19| while an emergency related to substance use is someone experiencing an overdose.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1699)|
| 0:28:23| But what is an emergency relative to homelessness?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1703)|
| 0:28:25| For the person experiencing homelessness, it's that moment when they lose their housing.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1705)|
| 0:28:29| All the other emergency calls from people experiencing homelessness are about a physical, mental health,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1709)|
| 0:28:34| or substance use emergency that's been exacerbated by the experience of living in shelter| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1714)|
| 0:28:38| or a place not meant for habitation.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1718)|
| 0:28:41| BMC, we've used both mobile crisis and the co-response unit for mental health emergencies.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1721)|
| 0:28:48| The co-response units are great.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1728)|
| 0:28:49| They're well-trained.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1729)|
| 0:28:50| They're compassionate.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=1730)|

| 1:40:47| which is our parent nonprofit.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6047)|
| 1:40:49| CAHOOTS operates a mobile integrated health model| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6049)|
| 1:40:54| in the communities of Eugene and our sister city across the highway, Springfield.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6054)|
| 1:41:00| And the CAHOOTS model consists of a crisis worker and a medic| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6060)|
| 1:41:08| on a van, a large sprinter van,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6068)|
| 1:41:12| that has the capability for transportation of clients as well.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6072)|
| 1:41:16| So, in Eugene, we strive to provide 36 hours of service in a 24-hour period.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6076)|
| 1:41:24| So that looks like one van being available 24 hours a day,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6084)|
| 1:41:28| and between the hours of 11 a.m. and 11 p.m.,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6088)|
| 1:41:32| a second van on the streets to provide extra coverage,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6092)|
| 1:41:36| as we have found that statistically those are the boundaries of our peak hours.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6096)|
| 1:41:41| In the city of Springfield, we also provide 24-hour coverage in that city as well.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6101)|
| 1:41:49| So, we respond to all sorts of calls.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6109)|
| 1:41:55| In our community, we are the third branch of public safety,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6115)|
| 1:41:59| so we have police, we have fire, EMS, and we also have CAHOOTS.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6119)|
| 1:42:05| The types of calls that we respond to really run the gamut of mental and physical health.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6125)|
| 1:42:13| So, this can be welfare checks, wound care, basic first aid, we take vitals,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6133)|
| 1:42:19| we check blood sugars, we respond to family disputes,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6139)|
| 1:42:23| we respond to individuals who are experiencing all sorts of crisis,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6143)|
| 1:42:28| including suicidal ideation or homicidal ideation,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6148)|
| 1:42:31| as well as providing death notifications when those events emerge.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6151)|
| 1:42:40| The average call volume that we've seen over the past three years| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6160)|
| 1:42:45| has been about 16,500 calls per year,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6165)|
| 1:42:50| and the teams that we have are dispatched from our local public safety answering point.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6170)|
| 1:42:58| So, there's a couple of different ways that a person can receive our services| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6178)|
| 1:43:05| or different ways that we'll end up showing up on scene.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6185)|
| 1:43:09| A person can call 9-1-1, a person can call 9-8-8,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6189)|
| 1:43:14| a person can also call the police department non-emergency line.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6194)|
| 1:43:19| And so, there's no wrong door to be able to access our services.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6199)|
| 1:43:23| Now, once one of those calls comes in, it goes to dispatch,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6203)|
| 1:43:29| and the dispatcher will collect all the information that they need| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6209)|
| 1:43:36| about what's going on on the scene, and it's at the point of dispatch| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6216)|
| 1:43:40| that the appropriate resource is decided.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6220)|
| 1:43:44| So, either we will be sent solo or sometimes in conjunction with the dispatcher.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6224)|
| 1:43:51| Sometimes in conjunction with a police response and or a fire response.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6231)|
| 1:43:58| A classic example here is in the event of a suicide,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6238)|
| 1:44:02| where the police will respond to that incident for a death investigation,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6242)|
| 1:44:09| and we will also be responding to take up the crisis side| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6249)|
| 1:44:15| for any individuals, family, friends, etc. that may also be on scene| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-240125-public-hearing?start=6255)|
